msg:The first time I went to Wuxi was because of Alec Su's concert. I checked online and found that Crowne Plaza Taihu was very close to the stadium where the concert was held, so I chose it decisively. I didn't expect it to be so convenient.

Location: Take Metro Line 4 to the Sports Center, exit at Exit 1, then turn left and walk along the MixC, and you will see the hotel.

Environment: The hotel has a good environment. As soon as you enter the lobby, you will smell a faint fragrance. It smells good.

Service: The service is very good. Check-in is very fast. Whether it is the front desk staff or the hotel security, the porter, etc., the service is very serious. I especially want to praise Yuris. The day before I checked in, she called me in person to ask me what requirements I had for the room, and then added WeChat to recommend attractions and restaurants in Wuxi to me. Thumbs up.

After entering the room, it may be because our room is facing west, so the room is very hot, and the air conditioner is not cooling, so I found Yuris on WeChat. She immediately asked the engineering depar**ent to take a look, and personally asked the room attendant to open the refrigerator for us and give us free drinks in the refrigerator. Thank you! Thank you!
When I checked out today, the front desk gave me a drink and a fridge magnet. I give you 100 points for your service.

Facilities: The facilities in the room are good, and the room is also very large, especially there is a large walk-in closet. From the room, you can see, I don’t know if it is Taihu Lake or Lihu Lake.

Hygiene: The room is very clean, every corner is very clean.
This time we checked in and also gave us a drink from the lobby bar, thank you!
The breakfast is very good, with a wide variety, a combination of Chinese and Western, basically everything; there is also a Family Mart in the hotel, the service is really good
If I have the opportunity to travel to Wuxi in the future, my first choice will still be to stay at Crowne Plaza Taihu

msg:Wuxi is a warm city, especially when we stayed at the Crowne Plaza Taihu Lake, which is a warmer place.
I have to mention the hotel staff Rita, who contacted me in advance the day before we checked in and asked us what we wanted for the room. When she learned that we were here for tourism, she sent me a travel guide to Wuxi and recommendations for popular restaurants, which was really useful for us who came to Wuxi for the first time.

Facilities: The hotel is in a good location, next to the stadium, and convenient for subway travel. There is also a MixC shopping mall next to it, which is very convenient for shopping and eating. The hotel facilities are also very complete, especially the sound of the TV can be projected into the bathroom, and you can watch movies immersively while taking a bath, and it is also a three-dimensional surround sound, which is great. The hotel's swimming pool is also very nice, the water is very clean, and for swimming enthusiasts, it is great to go swimming at any time during your stay. The hotel's breakfast is varied and delicious, especially pancakes and sesame paste, which is rare in other hotel breakfasts. There is also coffee for breakfast in the hotel, which is not only delicious, but also very user-friendly. There are two coffee machines in the restaurant, one for guests eating in the store, and the other is placed near the door of the restaurant, so that guests can pack a cup of coffee to take away after eating. For a heavy coffee lover, this is undoubtedly too heartwarming!

Hygiene: When traveling with children, the hotel must be clean and hygienic. The hygiene of this hotel has always been very good, and it is very reassuring to stay.

Service: The overall staff of the hotel are great, warm reception, and answer various questions and provide help, making people feel at home, very warm. Rita is very attentive. After seeing us check in, she took the initiative to ask if there are any items in the room that need to be replenished, and took the initiative to send us a few bottles of water. I have to say that such thoughtful service is very touching. It makes people feel at home while traveling.

This stay experience is perfect. When I come to Wuxi in the future, I will still stay in Crown. I would like to thank all the staff of the hotel.

前台check in速度也很快，小姐姐特別温柔，還給免費升級了房間，記得上次是32樓，這次入住的是37樓，房間也和上次的一模一樣，實在太有感覺了。
早餐6:30就開始了，菜品還是一樣的豐富，還有無錫小籠，看到還有煎餅果子，有些意外呀。必須説一下服務員特別好。
4樓就是健身房，還有游泳池，人不是很多，環境也可以。
下次來無錫還會首選這家。

msg:這個酒店的硬件，一點不值得這價格！八百左右一間房，在這個位置周邊啥也沒，並且大堂居然就衹有如圖這樣兩個小沙發！排隊辦理入住，長者小孩沒地方坐，旁邊的飲品店坐了一下服務員立馬就去趕人，太尷尬了！網上圖片的大堂都是隔壁飲品店，和酒店沒關係。
沒有電動窗簾智能馬桶，老式馬桶很難按壓，這些就算了，房卡反應遲鈍，每次都是反覆插卡拔卡，第二天實在忍受不了打電話，客服告知往下轉開不了再上轉，第一次遇到這樣的。更鬱悶的是洗手枱還能下不去水！游泳池很小，衹有三個泳道，還有教練和外面上課的孩子在裏面。房間送的水是冰露礦泉水。早餐種類也非常少。真是一點像五星級酒店。
送的飲品券，真的還是別那麼寒磣了，勾兑的飲料倒入一次性紙杯，真是不夠費事。我腸胃差，喝了橙汁之後腹瀉跑廁所三次，真的還不如不送。
真是覺得對不起這個價格。住過的酒店沒有性價比這樣的。對於接觸到的服務人員，還是挺滿意，但是硬件真的太差了。

msg:先説好的吧 這家酒店很在乎客人評價 這也是好事 
服務比較熱情 工作人員都比較客氣 需要什麼東西送來的也很及時 

因為入住發生了些不愉快（健身房理直氣壯不允許三歲小孩帶游泳圈游泳） 值班經理當晚及時處理 並贈送了行政酒廊權益 酒廊的工作人員Lily服務熱情周到 好評 

再説失望的吧 酒店確實比較老了 牆紙補的補 脱落的脱落 最失望就是健身房 游泳池 聽説是外包給第三方的 管理混亂 居然不讓三歲小孩帶游泳圈進去 説是擔心側翻（這是什麼奇葩理由? 如果99.99999%的酒店都沒有這個規定 你們應該想一下這條是否合理 你們想為自己的規定辯護肯定有各種各樣的理由 問題是你們做的也不像説的這麼重視安全 裏面的救生員一直低頭玩手機喝茶 聊天 ….） 這個健身房衞生水平應該五星級酒店墊底的水平 ….

酒店服務人員值班經理態度確實很好的 解決問題也及時 不給差評 親子旅遊不推薦

我們是週四（3月16日）晚上快11點的時候到達酒店的，前台的Linda（如果沒記錯名字的話）小姐姐態度很好，還幫忙升級了房型。週五晚餐是在中餐廳，菜品的味道不錯，擺盤好看，服務也非常熱情。

不足：我們是開車去的無錫，酒店地庫的停車場和地庫進酒店的廊廳有點味道，而且居然關燈了，這應該是我第一次遇到五星酒店從停車場進入的時候沒有燈光。
週五（3月17日）傍晚6點多回酒店，本來打算車停在酒店門口讓家人先下的。剛停好車居然保安和一個穿西裝的（可能是大堂經理？不確定）就過來叫我停到地下去別停地面，這也是第一次遇到居然不是來幫忙開門拿行李而是趕着走的😂。由於是帶着小朋友出來玩，所以也就懶得計較，就直接開走了。
